GT Equivalence Verification (BPG12)

GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P
Candidate formulas: 62

GT (fixed):  
\[
0.8770002846\,P\sin(0.5671736066\,t)\;+\;0.7013915187(1-P/65.7541311409)P
\]
Expand the polynomial part:
\[
0.7013915187P - \frac{0.7013915187}{65.7541311409}P^2
\]
So GT has exactly:
- a \(P\sin(\omega t)\) term with \(\omega=0.5671736066\) and coefficient \(0.8770002846\),
- a linear-in-\(P\) term,
- a quadratic-in-\(P\) term,
- **no** constant term, no \(\cos\) term, no \(|P|\), no logs/exp, no extra \(t\)-only terms.

Thus any matching candidate must be reducible (by parameter choices) to:
\[
(\text{const})P^2 + (\text{const})P + (\text{const})P\sin(\omega t)
\]
with the correct \(\omega\), and with all other structures eliminated.

---

### 1. \(P^2c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\cos(c3 t+c4) + c5\sin(Pc6+c7)\)
The last term depends on \(P\) inside sine and is not in GT; set \(c5=0\) to remove it. Then we still have a \(P\cos(\cdot)\) term, but GT needs \(P\sin(\omega t)\). A cosine can become sine via phase shift: \(\cos(\theta-\pi/2)=\sin\theta\). So choose \(c4=-\pi/2\), \(c3=0.5671736066\), \(c2=0.8770002846\). Choose \(c1=0.7013915187\), \(c0=-0.7013915187/65.7541311409\). Works. **Match.**

### 2. \(P^2c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\cos(c3 t+c4)\)
Same as (1) without the extra sine-in-\(P\) term. Use the same parameter choices as above. **Match.**

### 3. \(P^2c0 + P^2c1 + Pc2 + Pc3\cos(c4 t+c5) + Pc6\)
Combine like terms: \(P^2(c0+c1) + P(c2+c6) + P c3\cos(\cdot)\). This can match GT by setting \(c3\cos\) to sine via phase shift and choosing sums to equal the needed coefficients. Always possible (free parameters). **Match.**

### 4. \(P^2c0 + Pc1 + Pc2\sin(c3 + c4 t)\)
Already has \(P\sin(\text{affine in }t)\). Set \(c3=0\), \(c4=0.5671736066\), \(c2=0.8770002846\), \(c1=0.7013915187\), \(c0=-0.7013915187/65.7541311409\). **Match.**

### 5. \(P^2c0 + Pc1\sin(c2+c3 t) + Pc4 + Pc5\)

### 6. \(P^2c0 + P^2c1 + Pc2 + Pc3\sin(c4 t+c5)\)
